# Platforms State of the Union

## Summary
2018 Platforms State of the Union

## Info
* Featured
* WWDC 2018 - Session 102 - iOS, macOS, tvOS, watchOS
* https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/

of](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=265) [each.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=266) [Now, we don't require users to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=268) [sign into Maps but instead we](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=270) [use rotating random identifiers](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=272) [that can't be tied to an Apple](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=274) [ID to enable relevant results.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=276) [We use on-device intelligence to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=279) [enable powerful features like](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=281) [search and memories in photos](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=283) [without analyzing photos in the](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=286) [cloud.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=290) [We designed Face ID so all Face](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=290) [ID data is encrypted, protected](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=293) [by the Secure Enclave and](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=295) [doesn't ever leave your device.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=296) [And when we collect users' data](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=299) [And when we collect users' data](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=299) [or allow a third party to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=301) [collect data like photos, we](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=303) [make sure we do so with the](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=305) bit](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=307) [deeper into transparency and](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=309) [control.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=311) [You have all seen these alerts](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=312) [when you request access to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=314) [location or photos.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=316) [And this alert includes a](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=318) [purpose string.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=320) [Now this is what you provide in](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=321) [order to explain why you're](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=323) [requesting data and how you will](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=325) [use that data.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=327) [Now a good string includes a](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=329) [clear explanation of what](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=331) [features it will enable and what](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=332) [functionality it will improve.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=336) [Now, the more specific you are](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=339) [with your users, the more likely](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=342) [they are to grant you access.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=344) [We think it's critically](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=347) [important to understand and for](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=348) [users to understand how their](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=351) [data will be used.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=353) [So app review is paying closer](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=354) [attention to these purpose](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=356) [strings.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=358) [So if you have a purpose string](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=359) [So if you have a purpose string](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=359) [like this, which you know, it's](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=361) [clearly not valid, you may get](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=363) [dinged by app review.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=365) [Now this string technically](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=366) [explains how data will be used.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=370) [But it lacks detail so it's](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=372) [really hard for your user to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=375) [make a decision.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=377) [Now some users may have concerns](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=380) [about granting your app](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=382) [microphone access but it may be](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=384) [key to your app's functionality.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=387) [So that's why it's important to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=390) [have a clear purpose string like](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=391) [this one that explains exactly](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=393) [how you are going to use the](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=395) [data.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=399) [Now great features don't have to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=399) [be at the expense of privacy.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=401) [But instead can support them by](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=403) [making it clear to users how](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=405) [you're going to protect their](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=407) about](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=414) [security.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=415) [And in order to again.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=449) [Now in CloudKit in the cloud,](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=451) debug and trace](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=804) [through our code but we all know](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=805) [that it's slow.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=807) [And so two years ago, we brought](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=808) [you this new API called os log.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=810) [It's an efficient and performant](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=812) [API that captures logs and](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=814) [tracepoints across all levels of](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=816) [the system.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=818) [It's fast and [year builds on top of os log and](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=825) [it's called os signpost.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=827) [It's a powerful technique that](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=830) [provides rich, contextual data](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=831) [for your application in a format](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=833) [that instruments can interpret.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=835) [So you could use signpost Xcode.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1341) [And finally, we're introducing](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1344) [the concept of notarized apps.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1345) [This is an extension to the](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1348) [Developer ID program for apps](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1350) [that are distributed outside of](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1352) [the Mac App Store.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1353) [And it has two main goals.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1354) [The first is to detect malware](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1356) [even faster than today before it](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1358) [gets distributed to our users.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1360) [And second, provide a](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1362) [finer-grained revocation](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1363) [capability so that we can revoke](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1365) [a specific version of a](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1366) [compromised app as opposed to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1368) [revoking the entire signing](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1370) [certificate.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1372) [Now here's how it works.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1373) [You develop the bug and build](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1375) [your app as before.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1376) [And you sign it with your](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1377) [Developer ID Certificate.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1379) [Developer ID Certificate.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1379) [But before distributing it to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1381) [your users, you submit to the](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1382) [Developer ID Notary Service.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1384) [Once notarized, you distribute](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1386) [the app through your existing](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1388) [channel.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1389) [Once your user runs the app on](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1391) [their system, MacOS Mojave will](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1393) [check with the Notary Service to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1395) [make sure the app is properly](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1396) [notarized and is not known to be](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1398) [malicious.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1400) [Now, the service is not app](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1402) [review.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1404) [There are no new guidelines](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1405) [being imposed on Developer ID](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1406) [apps as a result of the Notary](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1407) [Service.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1409) [It is used exclusively to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1410) [analyze apps for security](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1412) [purposes.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1414) [A future version of MacOS will](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1415) [require all Developer ID apps to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1417) [be notarized by the service](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1420) [before they can be installed so](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1421) [we want you to get ready.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1423) [It's available in beta today.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1424) [We encourage you to try it out](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1426) [and give us feedback.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1428) [And those are the enhancements](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1430) [to Gatekeeper in MacOS [Let's look at what you need to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1821) [do in your apps to support Dark](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1824) [Mode.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1826) [Because we want to make your](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1830) [applications, we are not](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=1831) command](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4507) [encoding.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4509) [Now historically, your app would](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4509) [encode its GPU commands using](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4511) [the CPU and then subsequently](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4513) [execute those commands on the](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4514) [GPU.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4516) [And while Metal enabled this](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4517) [encoding to be very fast, it](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4518) [could still become bottlenecked](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4520) [by the synchronization between](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4521) [the CPU and the GPU.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4523) [Well, now in iOS 12 and macOS](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4524) [Mojave, you can actually encode](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4526) [those commands right on the GPU](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4528) [itself, freeing up precious CPU](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4529) [time for other use by your games](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4532) [and apps.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4534) [And because you issue these](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4535) [commands right on the GPU using](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4536) [a compute shader, you can](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4538) [actually officially construct](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4539) ray tracing.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4597) [Now this is a time-honored](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4598) [technique to achieve incredibly](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4599) [realistic scenes, often used for](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4601) [high-end rendering and 3D](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4604) [product design.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4605) [However, it traditionally had to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4606) [be done offline because it was](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4608) [so computationally expensive.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4609) [Now let me describe why very](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4611) [quickly.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4614) [First, you would need to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4615) [mathematically model the rays](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4616) [from a light source as they](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4618) [bounce off of objects through](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4618) [bounce off of objects through](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4618) [the scene, toward the screen,](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4620) [and into your eye.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4622) [And to achieve higher and higher](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4624) [resolutions, you would need to](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4625) [add more, and more, and more](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4627) [rays until you could reach the](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4630) [desired resolution.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4634) [And this simple 1k-by-1k image](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4635) [would take nearly 6 million rays](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4637) [to generate.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4639) [Now each of those rays also must](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4640) [be processed with at least two](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4642) [sets of expensive mathematical](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4643) [calculations.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4644) [First, you had to determine if a](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4646) [given ray intersects a](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4647) [particular triangle in your](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4648) [scene.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4649) [And second, you must apply a](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4650) [material-specific shader](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4651) [necessary to generate the pixel.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4653) [Now originally, both of these](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4655) [operations would have been](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4657) [performed by the CPU.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4658) [But while the GPU can easily](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4659) [handle the pixel shading, the](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4661) [ray-triangle intersection itself](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4663) [could remain an expensive CPU](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4665) [bottleneck, and it would be](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4666) [incredibly difficult to move](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4667) [this to the GPU efficiently.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4669) [But the new Metal Ray-Triangle](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4671) [Intersector solves this problem](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4672) [for you.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4674) [And with this new API, you get a](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4675) [dramatic increase in performance](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4676) [of up to 10x in a very](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4678) [of up to 10x in a very](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4678) [simple-to-use package, all](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4680) [pre-optimized for use with our](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4681) [iOS and macOS GPUs.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4683) [And it really is that simple,](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4686) [just a few lines of code.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4687) [And the ray tracing, like many](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4689) [GPU compute operations, is](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4692) [exactly the kind of operation](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4693) [that can efficiently scale with](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4695) [the available GPU horsepower.](https://developer.apple.com/videos/wwdc2018/videos/play/wwdc2018/102/?time=4696) [So we can actually get even
